Aqua Aerobics

- Outdoor Family Area

## KidsPoolParties

Doyour kids love the water? If you're looking for birthday venues foryour child's next swimming party, our centreoffersoneof thebestvenuesintown!

Take thehassleout of yourchildren'sbirthdayparty and enjoy aswimmingparty at ourcentre.

## KidsPoolPartyWill Include:

Yourchildren's birthdayparty willinvolve lots of laughs and fun guaranteed for thekids.Plus,no stress for theparents!Allguestsarewelcometostayandenjoythecentre'sfacilities afteryourbirthdaypartyunder parent/guardian supervision.

We offer services to ensure you enjoy a fun, hassle free children's birthday party including:

- Party planning
- A fun and safe birthday party
- Fun pool games
- Best of all, we clean up the mess!

## Kids PoolParty Requirements

Minimum of 12 participants are required for allparties, including the child who's swimming party is it. All participantsmustbe5yearsorolderandbeconfidentinthewater.

Birthdaypartiescanbe alotof workbut apoolparty atourcentreisabreeze.We'llensure thekidshave a blast withfunpool games toplayandbest of all we'll takecareof theclean-up.Pleasenotefood will not be cutlery.

## Welcome to WaterMarc Banyule

Our multi-activity facility proudly serves the Greensborough community and surrounding areas, offering inclusive access to gym, group exercise classes, Learn to Swim programs, and a wide range of health and wellness services for people of all ages and abilities. 

Designed for the whole family, our centre features an expansive 850m2 gym, a vibrant pool hall with an Olympic-sized 50-metre pool, leisure and warm water pools, spa, sauna, and steam room. We also offer group exercise classes, including Reformer Pilates, and exciting aquatic attractions like our splash park and two giant waterslides. 

[Opening Hours](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/venue/opening-hours/) [Facilities](/venue/about-us/) [Christmas/New Year Opening Hours](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/wp-content/uploads/sites/86/2025/12/Merry-Xmas.jpg)

#### Learn to Swim

Learning to swim is an essential life skill. Learn more about our swimming and water safety program.

[learn more](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/learn-to-swim/goswim-swimming-lessons/)

#### Reformer Pilates

Discover our brand-new Reformer Pilates studio, offering dynamic, low-impact classes that build strength, flexibility, and balance in a welcoming, state-of-the-art space.

[learn more](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/reformer-pilates/)

#### Gym

Train your way in our fully equipped 850m² gym, featuring 24/7 access, a functional training zone, and a dedicated recovery area available during staffed hours.

[learn more](/gym/)

## Page 2: https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/

# Swim at WaterMarc Banyule

## Make a splash in our aquatic space

At WaterMarc Banyule we offer a range of aquatic facilities and programs to help our community keep active and feel safe around the water.

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aquatic-facilities/)

#### Aquatic Facilities

There is something for everyone to enjoy our aquatic facilities all year round.

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aquatic-facilities/)

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/lap-lane-availability/)

#### Lap Lane Availability

We aim to have at least two lap swimming lanes available to the public during all pool opening hours Monday to Sunday (subject to event bookings).

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/lap-lane-availability/)

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aqua-aerobics/)

#### Aqua Aerobics

Aqua aerobics classes offer you a great way to stay fit without aggravation or risking injury. See our timetable for classes.

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aqua-aerobics/)

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/squads/)

#### Squads

Our squads program supports all swimmers to train to their individual potential and maximise their enjoyment of the sport, whether swimming for fun, competition and other aquatic activities.

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/squads/)

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aquatic-supervision/)

#### Aquatic Supervision

Parents/Guardians must actively supervise their children when in our venue. If you are not confident in the water or not a strong swimmer, please let our staff know as you enter the facility. 

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aquatic-supervision/)

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aquatic-capacity-procedure/)

#### Aquatic Capacity Procedure

We have aquatic capacity procedures in place for events or hot weather, where we expect a high volume of guests looking to use our pool and aquatic areas.

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/swim/aquatic-capacity-procedure/)

###### Learn to swim

Our GOswim Swimming and Water Safety Program equips students of all ages and abilities with essential skills for life!

[Learn More](https://recreation-base-template.bcms-recreation.com/learn-to-swim/goswim-swimming-lessons/)

PLEASE NOTE: NO 24/7 ACCESS DUE TO REFURBISHMENT AND MAINTENANCE ISSUES .APOLOGIES FOR INCONVENIENCE CAUSED.

NEW GYM OPEN SATURDAY 20 DECEMBER FROM 7AM

## Page 4: https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/reformer-pilates/

# Reformer Pilates

## reformer pilates is now at watermarc!

**We’re excited to introduce Reformer Pilates at WaterMarc** **in our brand new studio!**

Reformer Pilates is a whole-body workout. Let our expert instructors guide you to improve your wellbeing in a supportive and welcoming environment. 

  * Dedicated Reformer Pilates studio for intimate classes
  * Increases general mobility
  * Adaptable to various fitness levels by easing or increasing resistance
  * Low impact, joint-friendly workouts
  * Qualified instructors



### Benefits of Reformer Pilates

**Improve Core Strength**

Reformer Pilates focuses heavily on engaging the core muscles, including abdominals, lower back and pelvic floor. Strengthening these muscles improves posture, stability and overall functional movement.

**Enhance Mobility**

Regular practice on the reformer helps improve both static and dynamic flexibility. The machine allows for controlled stretching and lengthening of muscles, promoting joint mobility and reducing stiffness.

**Better Posture**

Through targeted exercises, Reformer Pilates helps align the spine and strengthen postural muscles. This results in improved posture, which can alleviate back, neck and shoulder pain often caused by poor alignment. 

**Strengthen and Tone Muscles**

The resistance provided by the reformer machine allows for a full-body workout that targets all major muscle groups. It leads to increased muscle tone, strength and endurance – especially in the legs, arms and core.

**Low Impact Workout**

Unlike high-impact exercise, Reformer Pilates provides a low-impact workout that reduces stress on the joints while effectively strengthening and toning muscles. This may make it suitable for people with joint issues or those recovering from injury. Please note that those recovering from injuries will need a written clearance from their supervising medical practitioner before participating in our general classes.

**Improve Balance and Coordination**

The reformer machine encourages controlled movements that challenge your balance and awareness for self. This helps improve coordination, stability and overall movement efficiency.

**Injury Rehab and Prevention**

Reformer Pilates is often used for rehabilitation because it strengthens muscles in a safe and controlled manner, helping to prevent future injuries. The equipment can also be adapted for a range of abilities and injury concerns. Please note that those recovering from injuries will need a written clearance from their supervising medical practitioner before participating in our general classes.

**Practice Mindfulness**

Reformer Pilates can encourage us to slow down, concentrate on our body’s movements and flow through positions. This practice can help to reduce stress and encourage us to find calm and mental clarity.

### Why choose us?

We offer facilities designed to support your health and wellness journey. With a Reformer Pilates membership, you’ll enjoy access to all our facilities, plus unlimited Reformer Pilates classes each week.

  * **Mix up your workouts** : Choose from Reformer Pilates, group exercise classes or a gym session.
  * **Expert Instructors** : Our qualified team provides personalised support and guidance to help you achieve your goals.
  * **Welcoming Community** : Join a positive, inclusive environment that motivates and inspires you every step of the way. 
  * **Flexible Scheduling** : With a packed timetable of classes and membership options, getting active has never been easier.



[Join Now](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/join/memberships/)

###### _OUR TIMETABLE_

With over 30 Reformer Pilates classes each week, there’s always a session to fit your schedule. Enjoy unlimited access as a member and explore our full timetable to find your perfect class!

[View Timetable](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/wp-content/uploads/sites/86/2025/05/image-16-1.png)

### Frequently Asked Questions

****What is Reformer Pilates?** **

Reformer Pilates is a low-impact, full-body workout. The reformer is a bed-like machine that moves back and forward and features functionalities (i.e. springs) to increase resistance as you work out. 

****Do I need prior experience with Reformer Pilates?****

No prior experience is necessary. Our classes are designed for all fitness levels, and our instructors make sure to demonstrate techniques that are adaptable for beginners as well as experts. We strongly encourage you to arrive early if you are attending your first class and make yourself known to the instructor. This will ensure that you have the opportunity to familiarise yourself with the Reformer bed and allow the instructor time to answer any questions you may have and to discuss the upcoming class and equipment with you. 

****What should I bring to class?****

Wear comfortable workout clothing, bring a towel and water bottle. We provide all the equipment you’ll need.

****How long are the classes?****

Classes run for 45 minutes, ensuring a total body workout as well as a mindful practice.

******Is Reformer Pilates suitable for injuries or rehabilitation?******

Reformer Pilates is low-impact and great for rehabilitation. Let your instructor know about any injuries so they can tailor the workout for you. Please note that if you are recovering from an injury or are living with a chronic condition you will need to provide us with a written clearance from your supervising medical or allied health practitioner before participating in any of our general Reformer Pilates classes.

********Do I need to be flexible to try Reformer Pilates?********

Flexibility is not a requirement for Reformer Pilates rather Reformer Pilates helps improve flexibility over time. Exercises in Reformer Pilates can be modified to accommodate all most of flexibility.

**********Will Reformer Pilates help me lose weight?**********

While Reformer Pilates is not primarily a cardio workout, it can aid in weight loss by building lean muscle, boosting metabolism, and improving overall body composition.

************What are the benefits of Reformer Pilates over mat Pilates?************

Reformer Pilates uses the resistance of the machine to provide a deeper, more targeted workout, helping to strengthen muscles, improve alignment, and increase flexibility.

# About Us

## ******Our Story******

WaterMarc Banyule is the largest aquatic and leisure facility in Victoria’s northern region, offering you the best in swimming, fitness and fun. This multi-activity regional facility serves the Greensborough community and surrounding suburbs. You can experience advanced aquatic and leisure programs and facilities which caters for the inclusion of people of all ages and abilities.

A state-of-the-art leisure facility, WaterMarc provides a range of amenities for you to enjoy, including an indoor 50-metre Olympic swimming pool and Learn to Swim pool. Your little ones will become confident in and around the water whilst enjoying our leisure and toddler pools.

You can enjoy the health benefits of our warm water program pool, spa, sauna and steam room facilities. If adrenaline is more your pace, you will love the Tantrum Alley waterslide and swimming pool inflatable.

We offer group exercise classes which also include services for seniors, kids’ birthday parties and two exciting waterslides. We are the perfect place for our community to make new friends while working on your health and fitness.

WaterMarc is also the home to a Victoria first program, Immersion Therapy. Immersion Therapy is award-winning, and evidence based with services utilising SCUBA equipment to create unique, individualised experiences tailored to meet the diverse needs and goals of it’s participants.

Come in and visit us today! We look forward to providing you with the best health and fitness experiences possible.

### Our Facilities

#### Health Club

Our 850m2 state-of-the-art gym offers cardio, strength and weight areas to provide you with everything you need to find your space and work on your goals. We’re also excited to offer a massive Group Fitness studio, Cycle studio, Wellness studio and Functional Training room. 

[Learn More](/gym)

#### Aquatic

With an Olympic 50m pool, Leisure pool, Warm Water Pool, Spa, Sauna, Steam Room, giant Splash Park and two huge Waterslides, There is something for everyone to enjoy our aquatic facilities all year round.

[Learn More](/swim/)

#### Swimming Lessons

GOswim swimming and water safety lessons are a fun and engaging way for kids and adults to learn to swim and be safe in aquatic environments. Suitable for infants from 6 months of age through to adults.

[Learn More](/learn-to-swim/goswim-swimming-lessons/)

#### Group Exercise

Group Exercise classes are a great social way to help build your confidence, motivation and accountability whilst making you smile. Our timetable features classes ranging from strength-based through to wellness.

[Learn More](/gym/group-exercise/)

#### Accessibility

We aim to provide a welcoming and comfortable environment for people of all abilities. Our facilities, programs and services have been designed to allow people of all abilities to lead active and healthy lifestyles.

[Learn More](/venue/accessibility/)

#### Birthday Parties

[Learn More](/venue/birthday-parties/)

#### Childcare

# GOswim Swimming and Water Safety Program

## GOswim Swimming and Water Safety Program

#### Learn to swim with us!

WaterMarc Banyule is proud to deliver GOswim Swimming Lessons to students, families and the community in Greensborough and surrounding areas.  
  
GOswim lessons will equip students of all ages and abilities with essential swimming and water safety skills, focusing on five key learning areas:

  * Safe entries and exits 
  * Balance, movement and recovery 
  * Breath control, submersion and readiness 
  * Water safety 
  * Swimming stroke development



Enquire Now

### GOswim Lessons at WaterMarc Banyule

  * **Ages:** infants from 6 months of age through to adults
  * **Program runs for:** 48 Weeks
  * **Held in our:** heated indoor pool
  * Ongoing Membership with **exclusive benefits!**
  * Students can join a **small group class** or request **private one-on-one lessons**



**Waterslide access is now included in your GOswim Membership***

*Age, height and weight restrictions apply.

### GOswim Program

Developed in partnership with **Swimming Australia** , GOswim swimming and water safety lessons focus on contemporary and activity-based aquatic learning. GOswim is a fun and engaging way for everyone to learn to swim and stay safe in aquatic environments. Lessons empower participants to build confidence and improve swimming ability through exercises tailored to promote optimal development and competency.   
  
Students can progress at any time and will be awarded a medal upon level progression. 

### Overview of Learning Outcomes

  * Infants (6+ months)
  * Preschool (3+ years)
  * Children
  * GOswim Academy
  * Teens
  * Adults
  * All Abilities



#### Infants (6+ months)

Begin your child’s water safety journey from 6 months with GOswim sessions focused on water familiarisation. Parents or carers join their infants in the pool to learn essential skills in a fun, supportive environment.

  * Suitable for babies aged 6+ months (recommended to secure your enrolment from 5 months of age).
  * A Parent/Carer must be in the water with their infant for the entire lesson.



#### Preschool (3+ years)

Help your child build water confidence and independence. Lessons for preschool-aged children use fun, activity-based learning to teach safe entries and exits, breath control, and essential water safety skills.

  * Suitable for children aged 3+ years.
  * A parent or carer observes from poolside for the full lesson.



#### Children

Lessons for primary-aged children use a fun-filled and activity-based style of learning, focusing on the five key areas of learning:

  * Safe entries and exits 
  * Breath Control, Submersion and Readiness 
  * Balance, Movement and Recovery 
  * Stroke Development 
  * Water Safety 



#### GOswim Academy

GOswim Academy bridges the gap between learning swimming foundations and joining recreational or competitive squads. It encourages ongoing participation through school competitions, fitness swimming, and pathways into aquatic sports.

_GOswim Academy session availability may vary, please enquire to learn more._

#### Teens (13 – 17 years)

Help teens develop water safety awareness, build confidence, and improve swimming skills in a fun, social environment. Lessons are designed for teenage students and focus on essential skills, stroke development, fitness, and teamwork.

  * **TeenStart:** For beginners, building confidence and essential water safety skills. 
  * **TeenSkill:** For intermediate swimmers looking to improve stroke technique and endurance. 
  * **TeenActive:** For competent and confident swimmers looking to refine techniques, build fitness, and explore aquatic career pathways. 



__Teen lesson availability may vary, please enquire to learn more.__

#### Adults (18+ years)

It’s never too late to learn to swim or refine your technique. Develop water safety awareness, build confidence, improve swimming skills, and stay active in a calm, supportive environment. Lessons are designed for adult students (18+ years) and focus on essential skills, stroke development and fitness.

  * **AdultStart:** For beginners learning foundational skills like floating and breath control.
  * **AdultSkill:** For intermediate swimmers looking to improve stroke technique, breathing, and strength.
  * **AdultActive:** For competent and confident swimmers focusing on fun, fitness, endurance, and stroke efficiency.



_Adult lesson availability may vary, please enquire to learn more._

#### All Abilities

We welcome students of all abilities and ages to participate in our inclusive GOswim program. Our lessons can be easily modified and adapted to suit your specific needs, whether this may be a one-on-one lesson, extra time or other. If you are seeking an accessible swimming experience, please contact us to discuss.

Enquire Today

### Membership Inclusions

When you become a member of our GOswim program at WaterMarc Banyule, you’ll be accessing these great inclusions: 

  * Weekly lessons with easy and affordable payments
  * GOswim Welcome Bag to store your swim gear 
  * Unlimited student aquatic access outside of lessons 
  * 4 weeks of unlimited family swim access over summer 
  * 1-week Summer Holiday Swimming Program 
  * Active World App access to conveniently manage your membership
  * Waterslide Access**



Weekly lessons start at: $21.70

_*Membership terms and conditions apply._

**Age, weight and height restrictions apply.

Enquire Now

### Swimming lessons for all abilities

We welcome students of all abilities and ages to participate in our GOswim program. If you are seeking an accessible and inclusive swimming experience, please contact us to discuss.

enquire Today

### Start your GOswim Journey

Sometimes it’s easier to talk things through – especially if you’re enrolling multiple students or want advice on the right level. Our friendly team is ready to guide you and make the process simple.

Call us to speak with a team member or, complete the enquiry form below and we’ll get back to you.

[Call Us](tel:03%209422%206111)

#### Enrol via our app

Everyone’s GOswim journey is powered by innovative technology. Enrol in lessons via our Active World app. Follow the steps below:

  1. Download the [Active World app](https://qrco.de/bbRx0F)
  2. Create an account
  3. Tap **_Book Weekly Lesson_** from the home screen 
  4. Add each student you wish to enrol, if not yourself. Then simply follow the prompts to find a lesson and time that suits you.



If you need assistance, please complete the enquiry form on this page for a team member to give you a call back.

The Active World app was specifically designed to improve communication and interaction between our GOswim team and students, parents/carers. Your **self-managed** personal portal will enable you to:

  * View upcoming classes 
  * Book new classes 
  * Advise of us of student absence and book a make-up lesson
  * Track learning pathways, skill achievement and progression
  * Receive digital awards for effort, teamwork, perseverance and having FUN! 
  * Send and receive messages to the Centre staff 
  * Manage personal and billing details

# Gym

## Find ways to get active

At WaterMarc Banyule we offer a range of gym facilities and exercise programs to help our community get active. Starting small and adding activity to your day has many health and wellbeing benefits.

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/fitness-facilities/)

#### Fitness Facilities

We offer a wide variety of health and exercise facilities ensuring there is something for everyone to support you on your health and wellbeing journey.

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/fitness-facilities/)

#### Group Exercise

Group Exercise classes are a great social way to help build your confidence and accountability, our classes foster a great community environment that makes you feel welcome, excited and keeps you coming back for more. 

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/group-exercise/)

#### Functional Training

B Active Functional Training personalised group coaching sessions are developed with a results-driven approach to elevate your workout experience.

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/functional-training/)

[](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/personal-training/)

#### Personal Training

Experience a one-on-one coaching service provided by certified trainers, involving a designed customised exercise program tailored to individual goals, abilities, and preferences.

[Learn More](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/gym/personal-training/)

###### **_Become a member_**

We have a range of memberships to suit all fitness goals and budgets.  
Join our community today.

[Join Now](https://www.watermarcbanyule.com.au/join/memberships/)

# **Memberships**

## Membership Options

There are many benefits to being a member and staying active at WaterMarc Banyule. We offer a broad range of high quality, modern fitness spaces, including individual personal training, large free weights and cardio areas as well as a wide variety of Group Exercise classes.  
  
You can become a member of WaterMarc Banyule in a few clicks by starting a new membership online, simply choose a membership option below and follow the prompts through our Active World membership portal. Alternatively, you can visit WaterMarc Banyule where our team can help you get your new membership started.
